```
.toContain(), .toContainEqual()
  ğŸŸ¢ iterable
  ğŸŸ¢ '[1, 2, 3, 4]' contains '1'
  ğŸŸ¢ '["a", "b", "c", "d"]' contains '"a"'
  ğŸŸ¢ '[undefined, null]' contains 'null'
  ğŸŸ¢ '[undefined, null]' contains 'undefined'
  ğŸŸ¢ '[Symbol(a)]' contains 'Symbol(a)'
  ğŸŸ¢ '"abcdef"' contains '"abc"'
  ğŸŸ¢ '"11112111"' contains '"2"'
  ğŸŸ¢ 'Set {"abc", "def"}' contains '"abc"'
  ğŸŸ¢ '[0, 1]' contains '1'
  ğŸŸ¢ '[1n, 2n, 3n, 4n]' contains '1n'
  ğŸŸ¢ '[1, 2, 3, 3n, 4]' contains '3n'
  ğŸŸ¢ '[1, 2, 3]' does not contain '4'
  ğŸŸ¢ '[null, undefined]' does not contain '1'
  ğŸŸ¢ '[{}, []]' does not contain '[]'
  ğŸŸ¢ '[{}, []]' does not contain '{}'
  ğŸŸ¢ '[1n, 2n, 3n]' does not contain '3'
  ğŸŸ¢ error cases
  ğŸŸ¢ '[1, 2, 3, 4]' contains a value equal to '1'
  ğŸŸ¢ '["a", "b", "c", "d"]' contains a value equal to '"a"'
  ğŸŸ¢ '[undefined, null]' contains a value equal to 'null'
  ğŸŸ¢ '[undefined, null]' contains a value equal to 'undefined'
  ğŸŸ¢ '[Symbol(a)]' contains a value equal to 'Symbol(a)'
  ğŸŸ¢ '[{"a": "b"}, {"a": "c"}]' contains a value equal to '{"a": "b"}'
  ğŸŸ¢ 'Set {1, 2, 3, 4}' contains a value equal to '1'
  ğŸŸ¢ '[0, 1]' contains a value equal to '1'
  ğŸŸ¢ '[{"a": "b"}, {"a": "c"}]' does not contain a value equal to'{"a": "d"}'
  ğŸŸ¢ error cases for toContainEqual
```

### ğŸŸ¢Â <a id="user-content-r0s279" href="#r0s279">packages/jest-fake-timers/src/__tests__/legacyFakeTimers.test.ts</a>
```
FakeTimers construction
  ğŸŸ¢ installs setTimeout mock
  ğŸŸ¢ accepts to promisify setTimeout mock
  ğŸŸ¢ installs clearTimeout mock
  ğŸŸ¢ installs setInterval mock
  ğŸŸ¢ installs clearInterval mock
  ğŸŸ¢ mocks process.nextTick if it exists on global
  ğŸŸ¢ mocks setImmediate if it exists on global
  ğŸŸ¢ mocks clearImmediate if setImmediate is on global
FakeTimers runAllTicks
  ğŸŸ¢ runs all ticks, in order
  ğŸŸ¢ does nothing when no ticks have been scheduled
  ğŸŸ¢ only runs a scheduled callback once
  ğŸŸ¢ cancels a callback even from native nextTick
  ğŸŸ¢ cancels a callback even from native setImmediate
  ğŸŸ¢ doesnt run a tick callback if native nextTick already did
  ğŸŸ¢ doesnt run immediate if native setImmediate already did
  ğŸŸ¢ native doesnt run immediate if fake already did
  ğŸŸ¢ throws before allowing infinite recursion
FakeTimers runAllTimers
  ğŸŸ¢ runs all timers in order
  ğŸŸ¢ warns when trying to advance timers while real timers are used
  ğŸŸ¢ does nothing when no timers have been scheduled
  ğŸŸ¢ only runs a setTimeout callback once (ever)
  ğŸŸ¢ runs callbacks with arguments after the interval
  ğŸŸ¢ doesnt pass the callback to native setTimeout
  ğŸŸ¢ throws before allowing infinite recursion
  ğŸŸ¢ also clears ticks
FakeTimers advanceTimersByTime
  ğŸŸ¢ runs timers in order
  ğŸŸ¢ does nothing when no timers have been scheduled
```
